<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To create a controlled Carousel component, you can manage the state of the carousel using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">page</code> prop and update it
when the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onPageChange</code> event handler is called:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the carousel is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useCarousel</code> hook. This way
you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="autoplay" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#autoplay"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Autoplay</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">autoplay</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">loop</code> props to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Root</code> to make the carousel play automatically.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="pause-on-hover" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#pause-on-hover"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Pause on Hover</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This feature isn&#x27;t built-in, but you can use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">play()</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">pause()</code> methods from <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Context</code> to implement
pause on hover.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="thumbnail-indicators" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#thumbnail-indicators"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Thumbnail Indicators</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Replace default indicator dots with image thumbnails. Render each thumbnail inside <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Indicator</code> to create a
visual preview of each slide:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="vertical" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#vertical"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Vertical</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Add the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">orientation=&quot;vertical&quot;</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Root</code> to switch the carousel to vertical scrolling. This can be
helpful for displaying vertical galleries or content feeds.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="dynamic" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#dynamic"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Dynamic</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Manage slides dynamically by storing them in state and syncing the carousel page. Pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">page</code> prop and
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onPageChange</code> handler to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Root</code>, and update <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">slideCount</code> when slides are added or removed. This demonstrates
bidirectional state synchronization between your component state and the carousel.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="scroll-to-slide" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#scroll-to-slide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Scroll to Slide</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Context</code> to access the carousel API and call <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">api.scrollToIndex(index)</code> to programmatically navigate to a
specific slide. This is useful for creating custom navigation or jump-to-slide functionality.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="slides-per-page" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#slides-per-page"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Slides Per Page</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Display multiple slides simultaneously by setting the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">slidesPerPage</code> prop on <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Root</code>. Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">api.pageSnapPoints</code>
from <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Context</code> to render the correct number of indicators based on pages rather than individual slides. Add the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">spacing</code> prop to control the gap between slides.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="spacing" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#spacing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Spacing</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Control the gap between slides using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">spacing</code> prop on <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Root</code>. Combine it with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">slidesPerPage</code> to create
layouts that show partial previews of adjacent slides.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a7hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a7hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a7hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="variable-sizes" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#variable-sizes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Variable Sizes</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To allow slides with different widths, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">autoSize</code> prop on <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Root</code>. This lets each <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Item</code> define
its own width, and the carousel will adjust automatically. You can also use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">snapAlign</code> prop on individual items to
control where each one snaps into view.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_adhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_adhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_adhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;div&gt;</code> element.</p><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Prop</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Default</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Type</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">slideCount</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-minus icon icon--size_xs c_fg.muted" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 12h14"></path></svg></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">number</code><p class="text">The total number of slides.
Useful for SSR to render the initial ating the snap points.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">allowMouseDrag</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">false</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Whether to allow scrolling via dragging with mouse</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">asChild</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-minus icon icon--size_xs c_fg.muted" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 12h14"></path></svg></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior.</p><span class="text">For more details, read our<!-- --> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="link" href="/react/docs/guides/composition">Composition</a> <!-- -->guide.</span></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">autoplay</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">false</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm number</code><p class="text">Returns the current scroll progress as a percentage</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">getProgressText</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">() =&gt; string</code><p class="text">Returns the progress text</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">play</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">VoidFunction</code><p class="text">Function to start/resume autoplay</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">pause</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">VoidFunction</code><p class="text">Function to pause autoplay</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">isInView</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(index: number) =&gt; boolean</code><p class="text">Whether the item is in view</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">refresh</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">VoidFunction</code><p class="text">Function to re-compute the snap points
and clamp the page</p></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"carousel\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cCarousel.Root\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger /\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger /\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Item /\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Indicator /\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n\u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/react/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root className={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length}\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n          {images.map((image, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cCarousel.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n              \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup className={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n        {images.map((_, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCarousel.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} key={index} index={index} /\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/solid/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root class={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length}\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n          \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e\n            {(image, index) =\u003e (\n              \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} index={index}\u003e\n                \u003cimg src={image().src} alt={image().alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n              \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Index\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e{(_, index) =\u003e \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} index={index} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/vue/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :slide-count=\"images.length\"\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup :class=\"styles.ItemGroup\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Item v-for=\"(image, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n          \u003cimg :src=\"image.src\" :alt=\"image.alt\" width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup :class=\"styles.IndicatorGroup\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Indicator v-for=\"(_, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Indicator\" :index=\"index\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript\u003e\n  import { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/svelte/carousel'\n  import ArrowLeftIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/arrow-left'\n  import ArrowRightIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/arrow-right'\n  import styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\n  const images = [\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cCarousel.Root class={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length}\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n      {#each images as image, index}\n        \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} {index}\u003e\n          \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n    {#each images as _, index}\n      \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} {index} /\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n\u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nTo create a controlled Carousel component, you can manage the state of the carousel using the `page` prop and update it\nwhen the `onPageChange` event handler is called:\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/react/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [page, setPage] = useState(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root className={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length} page={page} onPageChange={(e) =\u003e setPage(e.page)}\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n          {images.map((image, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cCarousel.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n              \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup className={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n        {images.map((_, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCarousel.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} key={index} index={index} /\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/solid/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [page, setPage] = createSignal(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root\n      class={styles.Root}\n      slideCount={images.length}\n      page={page()}\n      onPageChange={(details) =\u003e setPage(details.page)}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n          \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e\n            {(image, index) =\u003e (\n              \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} index={index}\u003e\n                \u003cimg src={image().src} alt={image().alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n              \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Index\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e{(_, index) =\u003e \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} index={index} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/vue/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\nconst page = ref(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cdiv\u003eCurrent page: {{ page }}\u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model:page=\"page\" :slide-count=\"images.length\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup :class=\"styles.ItemGroup\"\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.Item v-for=\"(image, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n            \u003cimg :src=\"image.src\" :alt=\"image.alt\" width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup :class=\"styles.IndicatorGroup\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Indicator v-for=\"(_, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Indicator\" :index=\"index\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript\u003e\n  import { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/svelte/carousel'\n  import ArrowLeftIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/arrow-left'\n  import ArrowRightIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/arrow-right'\n  import styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\n  const images = [\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n  ]\n  let page = $state(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003eCurrent page: {page}\u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Root class={styles.Root} bind:page slideCount={images.length}\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        {#each images as image, index}\n          \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} {index}\u003e\n            \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n      {#each images as _, index}\n        \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} {index} /\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the carousel is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useCarousel` hook. This way\nyou can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel, useCarousel } from '@ark-ui/react/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const carousel = useCarousel({ slideCount: images.length })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003ePage: {carousel.page}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={carousel}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n            {images.map((image, index) =\u003e (\n              \u003cCarousel.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n                \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n              \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n            ))}\n          \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup className={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n          {images.map((_, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cCarousel.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} key={index} index={index} /\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel, useCarousel } from '@ark-ui/solid/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const carousel = useCarousel({ slideCount: images.length })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003ePage: {carousel().page}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={carousel}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n            \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e\n              {(image, index) =\u003e (\n                \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} index={index}\u003e\n                  \u003cimg src={image().src} alt={image().alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n                \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/Index\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n          \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e{(_, index) =\u003e \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} index={index} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Carousel, useCarousel } from '@ark-ui/vue/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nconst carousel = useCarousel({ slideCount: images.length })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003ePage: {{ carousel.page }}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"carousel\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup :class=\"styles.ItemGroup\"\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.Item v-for=\"(image, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n            \u003cimg :src=\"image.src\" :alt=\"image.alt\" width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup :class=\"styles.IndicatorGroup\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Indicator v-for=\"(_, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Indicator\" :index=\"index\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript\u003e\n  import { Carousel, useCarousel } from '@ark-ui/svelte/carousel'\n  import ArrowLeftIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/arrow-left'\n  import ArrowRightIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/arrow-right'\n  import styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\n  const images = [\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n  ]\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const carousel = useCarousel({\n    id,\n    defaultPage: 0,\n    slideCount: images.length,\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003ePage: {carousel().page}\u003c/output\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={carousel}\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        {#each images as image, index}\n          \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} {index}\u003e\n            \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n      {#each images as _, index}\n        \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} {index} /\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Autoplay\n\nPass the `autoplay` and `loop` props to `Carousel.Root` to make the carousel play automatically.\n\n**Example: autoplay**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/react/carousel'\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon, PauseIcon, PlayIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const Autoplay = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root className={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length} autoplay loop\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        {images.map((image, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCarousel.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n            \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control className={styles.Control} data-justify=\"center\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.AutoplayTrigger className={styles.AutoplayTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.AutoplayIndicator fallback={\u003cPlayIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cPauseIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.AutoplayIndicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.AutoplayTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/solid/carousel'\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon, PauseIcon, PlayIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const Autoplay = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root class={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length} autoplay loop\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e\n          {(image, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} index={index}\u003e\n              \u003cimg src={image().src} alt={image().alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control} data-justify=\"center\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.AutoplayTrigger class={styles.AutoplayTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cCarousel.AutoplayIndicator fallback={\u003cPlayIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cPauseIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.AutoplayIndicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.AutoplayTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/vue/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon, PauseIcon, PlayIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :slide-count=\"images.length\" autoplay loop\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup :class=\"styles.ItemGroup\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Item v-for=\"(image, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n        \u003cimg :src=\"image.src\" :alt=\"image.alt\" width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Control :class=\"styles.Control\" data-justify=\"center\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.AutoplayTrigger :class=\"styles.AutoplayTrigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.AutoplayIndicator\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate #fallback\u003e\u003cPlayIcon /\u003e\u003c/template\u003e\n          \u003cPauseIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.AutoplayIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.AutoplayTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript\u003e\n  import { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/svelte/carousel'\n  import ArrowLeftIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/arrow-left'\n  import ArrowRightIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/arrow-right'\n  import PauseIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/pause'\n  import PlayIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/play'\n  import styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\n  const images = [\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cCarousel.Root class={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length} autoplay loop\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n    {#each images as image, index}\n      \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} {index}\u003e\n        \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control} data-justify=\"center\"\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.AutoplayTrigger class={styles.AutoplayTrigger}\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.AutoplayIndicator\u003e\n        {#snippet fallback()}\u003cPlayIcon /\u003e{/snippet}\n        \u003cPauseIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.AutoplayIndicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.AutoplayTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Pause on Hover\n\nThis feature isn't built-in, but you can use the `play()` and `pause()` methods from `Carousel.Context` to implement\npause on hover.\n\n**Example: pause-on-hover**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/react/carousel'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const PauseOnHover = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root className={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length} autoplay loop\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Context\u003e\n          {({ isPlaying }) =\u003e (\n            \u003cspan className={styles.StatusText}\u003eAutoplay is: {isPlaying ? 'playing' : 'paused'}\u003c/span\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Carousel.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Context\u003e\n        {(api) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup\n            className={styles.ItemGroup}\n            onPointerOver={() =\u003e api.pause()}\n            onPointerLeave={() =\u003e api.play()}\n          \u003e\n            {images.map((image, index) =\u003e (\n              \u003cCarousel.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n                \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n              \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n            ))}\n          \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Carousel.Context\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup className={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n        {images.map((_, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCarousel.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} key={index} index={index} /\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/solid/carousel'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const PauseOnHover = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root class={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length} autoplay loop\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Context\u003e\n          {(carousel) =\u003e (\n            \u003cspan class={styles.StatusText}\u003eAutoplay is: {carousel().isPlaying ? 'playing' : 'paused'}\u003c/span\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Carousel.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Context\u003e\n        {(api) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup\n            class={styles.ItemGroup}\n            onPointerOver={() =\u003e api().pause()}\n            onPointerLeave={() =\u003e api().play()}\n          \u003e\n            \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e\n              {(image, index) =\u003e (\n                \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} index={index}\u003e\n                  \u003cimg src={image().src} alt={image().alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n                \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/Index\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Carousel.Context\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e{(_, index) =\u003e \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} index={index} /\u003e}\u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/vue/carousel'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :slide-count=\"images.length\" autoplay loop\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Context v-slot=\"api\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan :class=\"styles.StatusText\"\u003eAutoplay is: {{ api.isPlaying ? 'playing' : 'paused' }}\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Context v-slot=\"api\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup :class=\"styles.ItemGroup\" @pointerover=\"api.pause()\" @pointerleave=\"api.play()\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Item v-for=\"(image, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n          \u003cimg :src=\"image.src\" :alt=\"image.alt\" width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Context\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup :class=\"styles.IndicatorGroup\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Indicator v-for=\"(_, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Indicator\" :index=\"index\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript\u003e\n  import { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/svelte/carousel'\n  import styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\n  const images = [\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n    { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cCarousel.Root class={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length} autoplay loop\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(api)}\n        \u003cspan class={styles.StatusText}\u003eAutoplay is: {api().isPlaying ? 'playing' : 'paused'}\u003c/span\u003e\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Carousel.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(api)}\n      \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup\n        class={styles.ItemGroup}\n        onpointerover={() =\u003e api().pause()}\n        onpointerleave={() =\u003e api().play()}\n      \u003e\n        {#each images as image, index}\n          \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} {index}\u003e\n            \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/Carousel.Context\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n    {#each images as _, index}\n      \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} {index} /\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n\u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Thumbnail Indicators\n\nReplace default indicator dots with image thumbnails. Render each thumbnail inside `Carousel.Indicator` to create a\nvisual preview of each slide:\n\n**Example: thumbnail-indicator**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/react/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const ThumbnailIndicator = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root className={styles.Root} defaultPage={0} slideCount={images.length}\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n          {images.map((image, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cCarousel.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n              \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup className={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n        {images.map((image, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCarousel.Indicator className={styles.ThumbnailIndicator} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n            \u003cimg src={image.src} alt={image.alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/Carousel.Indicator\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/solid/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\nexport const ThumbnailIndicator = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cCarousel.Root class={styles.Root} slideCount={images.length}\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n          \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e\n            {(image, index) =\u003e (\n              \u003cCarousel.Item class={styles.Item} index={index}\u003e\n                \u003cimg src={image().src} alt={image().alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n              \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Index\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.IndicatorGroup class={styles.IndicatorGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={images}\u003e\n          {(image, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cCarousel.Indicator class={styles.ThumbnailIndicator} index={index}\u003e\n              \u003cimg src={image().src} alt={image().alt} width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/Carousel.Indicator\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.IndicatorGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Carousel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Carousel } from '@ark-ui/vue/carousel'\nimport { ArrowLeftIcon, ArrowRightIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/carousel.module.css'\n\nconst images = [\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/1/500/300', alt: 'Nature landscape' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/2/500/300', alt: 'City skyline' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/3/500/300', alt: 'Mountain view' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/4/500/300', alt: 'Ocean sunset' },\n  { src: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/5/500/300', alt: 'Forest path' },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCarousel.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :slide-count=\"images.length\"\u003e\n    \u003cCarousel.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cArrowLeftIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.ItemGroup :class=\"styles.ItemGroup\"\u003e\n        \u003cCarousel.Item v-for=\"(image, index) in images\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n          \u003cimg :src=\"image.src\" :alt=\"image.alt\" width=\"500\" height=\"300\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/Carousel.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cCarousel.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cArrowRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Carousel.NextTrigger\u003e\n
